# A ROS-O deb repository for jammy-one

## Install Instructions

```bash
echo "deb [trusted=yes] https://raw.githubusercontent.com/k-okada/ros-o-builder/jammy-one/repository// ./" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/k-okada_ros-o-builder-jammy-one.list
sudo apt update
sudo apt install python3-rosdep2
echo "yaml https://raw.githubusercontent.com/k-okada/ros-o-builder/jammy-one/repository//local.yaml debian" | sudo tee /etc/ros/rosdep/sources.list.d/1-k-okada_ros-o-builder-jammy-one.list
rosdep update

# install required packages, e.g.,
sudo apt install ros-one-desktop-full ros-one-plotjuggler ros-one-navigation [...]
```
